FROM (
    SELECT c.request_id, c.complaint_id, c.created_at, c.remarks, c.request_status_id, c.request_type_id, c.requested_by, c.reviewed_at, c.reviewed_by
    FROM complaint_requests AS c
    WHERE c.request_type_id = @requestTypeId_Value
    ORDER BY c.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @p2 OFFSET @p
) AS c1
INNER JOIN complaints AS c0 ON c1.complaint_id = c0.complaint_id
INNER JOIN request_types AS r ON c1.request_type_id = r.request_type_id
INNER JOIN request_statuses AS r0 ON c1.request_status_id = r0.request_status_id
INNER JOIN employees AS e ON c1.requested_by = e.employee_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON c1.reviewed_by = e0.employee_id
ORDER BY c1.created_at DESC

SELECT r0.role_request_id, r0.created_at, r0.current_role_id, r0.employee_id, r0.remarks, r0.request_status_id, r0.requested_role_id, r0.reviewed_at, r0.reviewed_by, e.employee_id, e.created_at, e.department_id, e.email, e.employee_name, e.is_active, e.mobile_number, e.password_hash, e.role_id, e.updated_at, r1.role_id, r1.created_at, r1.role_name, r2.role_id, r2.created_at, r2.role_name, r3.request_status_id, r3.status_name, e0.employee_id, e0.created_at, e0.department_id, e0.email, e0.employee_name, e0.is_active, e0.mobile_number, e0.password_hash, e0.role_id, e0.updated_at
FROM (
    SELECT r.role_request_id, r.created_at, r.current_role_id, r.employee_id, r.remarks, r.request_status_id, r.requested_role_id, r.reviewed_at, r.reviewed_by
    FROM role_requests AS r
    ORDER BY r.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r0
INNER JOIN employees AS e ON r0.employee_id = e.employee_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r1 ON r0.current_role_id = r1.role_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r2 ON r0.requested_role_id = r2.role_id
INNER JOIN request_statuses AS r3 ON r0.request_status_id = r3.request_status_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON r0.reviewed_by = e0.employee_id
ORDER BY r0.created_at DESC

FROM (
    SELECT r.role_request_id, r.created_at, r.current_role_id, r.employee_id, r.remarks, r.request_status_id, r.requested_role_id, r.reviewed_at, r.reviewed_by
    FROM role_requests AS r
    ORDER BY r.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS r0
INNER JOIN employees AS e ON r0.employee_id = e.employee_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r1 ON r0.current_role_id = r1.role_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r2 ON r0.requested_role_id = r2.role_id
INNER JOIN request_statuses AS r3 ON r0.request_status_id = r3.request_status_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON r0.reviewed_by = e0.employee_id
ORDER BY r0.created_at DESC
